# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/node--v22.13.0`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/node--v22.13.0$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/node--v22.13.0` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/node--v22.13.0`

# Node.js CommonJS to ESM Module Loader Migration Surface

## Your Task

Find all JavaScript and C++ source files in nodejs/node that implement the ESM loader and CJS-ESM interop bridge. Identify: the ModuleLoader class (lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js), the CJS loader's ESM fallback (finalizeEsmResolution in lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js), the ESM translators for different formats, the ESM specifier resolver, the ModuleJob linking/evaluation pipeline, the entry point ESM detection (run_main.js), and the native ModuleWrap C++ binding.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/node--v22.13.0.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/node--v22.13.0` (nodejs/node)

## Key Findings

**19 Core Files Identified:**

### JavaScript Files (ESM Loader)
- **loader.js**: ModuleLoader class managing resolution, loading, and job creation
- **module_job.js**: ModuleJob classes implementing linking and evaluation pipeline
- **module_map.js**: Caching infrastructure (ResolveCache, LoadCache)
- **translators.js**: Format-specific translators for module/commonjs/json/wasm
- **resolve.js**: ESM specifier resolution algorithm
- **load.js**: Source code loading from various protocols
- **get_format.js**: Module format detection
- **formats.js**: Extension-to-format mappings
- **utils.js**: Utility functions including compileSourceTextModule
- **hooks.js**: Custom loader hook system
- **initialize_import_meta.js**: import.meta initialization
- **create_dynamic_module.js**: Dynamic module creation
- **assert.js**: Import attribute validation
- **worker.js**: Worker thread support
- **shared_constants.js**: Shared constants
- **run_main.js**: Entry point detection and execution

### JavaScript Files (CJS Interop)
- **cjs/loader.js**: finalizeEsmResolution for ESM fallback

### C++ Files
- **src/module_wrap.cc**: ModuleWrap C++ implementation
- **src/module_wrap.h**: ModuleWrap C++ header

Key responsibilities include:\\n\\n- **Module resolution**: `resolve()` method (line 581) resolves module specifiers using either custom loader hooks or the default resolution algorithm\\n- **Module loading**: `load()` method loads module source code and metadata\\n- **Module job creation**: `getModuleJobForImport()` (line 241) creates or retrieves cached ModuleJob instances\\n- **Require integration**: `importSyncForRequire()` (line 291) handles require() calls to ESM modules from CommonJS\\n- **Custom loader hooks**: Managed through `setCustomizations()` (line 201) and the Hooks class\\n- **Caching**: Maintains `#resolveCache` and `loadCache` for efficient module resolution and loading\\n- **Translators**: Uses format-specific translators for different module types (module, commonjs, json, wasm)\\n\\n## Module Job and Linking/Evaluation Pipeline\\nThe **lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js** file implements the ModuleJob and ModuleJobSync classes that track module loading and linking:\\n\\n- **ModuleJob** (line 72): Tracks loading of a single module and its dependencies\\n  - `_link()` (line 114): Iterates module requests and links dependencies with the loader\\n  - `_instantiate()` (line 160): Instantiates all modules in the dependency graph\\n  - `run()` (line 262): Evaluates the module and handles evaluation-time errors\\n  - `instantiate()`: Public interface to trigger instantiation\\n- **ModuleJobBase** (line 60): Base class for ModuleJob and ModuleJobSync with shared properties (url, isMain, importAttributes)\\n- **ModuleJobSync** (line 310): Synchronous variant for handling require() of ESM modules in CommonJS\\n\\nThe linking pipeline:\\n1. Module resolution via `loader.resolve()`\\n2. Getting module requests via `module.getModuleRequests()`\\n3. Recursively linking all dependencies\\n4. Instantiating the module graph with `module.instantiate()`\\n5. Evaluating with `module.evaluate()`\\n\\n## Module Format and Resolution\\nFormat detection and resolution are handled by multiple files:\\n\\n- **lib/internal/modules/esm/get_format.js**: Determines ESM-loaded modules\\n\\n- Cross-references: When CommonJS calls `require()` on an ESM module, it goes through the cascaded loader\\n\\n## Dynamic Module Creation\\nThe Flow\\n1. **Entry point detection**: `executeUserEntryPoint()` \u2192 `shouldUseESMLoader()`\\n2. **Module request**: `import` statement or `import()` expression\\n3. **Resolution**: `ModuleLoader.resolve()` \u2192 `resolveESM()` in resolve.js\\n4. **Loading**: `ModuleLoader.load()` \u2192 reads source \u2192 detects format\\n5. **Translation**: Format-specific translator creates ModuleWrap\\n6. **Job creation**: `ModuleLoader.getModuleJobForImport()` \u2192 `ModuleJob` instance\\n7. **Linking**: `ModuleJob._link()` \u2192 recursively loads and links dependencies\\n8. **Instantiation**: `ModuleJob._instantiate()` \u2192 `module.instantiate()`\\n9. **Evaluation**: `ModuleJob.run()` \u2192 `module.evaluate()`\\n\\n## CJS Fallback for Ambiguous Files\\nWhen a .js file has no package.json type field:\\n1. First attempt CommonJS loading\\n2. If imports ESM syntax, retry with ESM\\n3. Uses content detection in `get_format.js`\\n4.
